<rating>5<//rating><Review>I've been here a number of times (lunch and dinner, over the past 3 years or so) and have always had a great experience. The decor isn't much to look at, but all of the food I've had has been extremely fresh and well-prepared. The buffet has a good variety, and all of the fresh veggies are beautiful. And you can't beat the price! Added bonus - I've got fairly serious food allergies, and the way they heat the food, it keeps your stuff on a single space on the griddle. I've been to other Mongolian places where they move the food across the whole griddle, so your stuff gets a lot of contamination from other peoples' plates, but here, your food stays on one section of the griddle until it is done.</Review>< Pics>

< text>
This is an outstanding Orthodontic office and I cannot say enough good things about them. ¬†The orthodontists and staff are very skilled and compassionate and the office staff is extremely competent and pleasant. All 3 of our children had a situation where their jaws were not growing properly. We went to two other orthodontists prior to going to Montano and Cardall and both of those offices recommended plan was to pull numerous teeth from my 3 children, use braces to straighten their teeth and then give them jaw surgery as young adults. After further research we found Montano and Cardall. Their recommended treatment was completely different. By using a Herbst appliance and braces, they were able to slowly encourage their jaws to grow and then used braces to align their teeth properly. After getting some surprising news that my case was going to be more in depth than the typical orthodontic case, I wasn‚Äôt sure what to do. I was informed along with braces I would also need to undergo two surgeries. This news was not fun to hear but I knew I needed to proceed. I never felt the need to get a second opinion because Dr. Montano and the staff made me feel comfortable and secure that my well being was in great hands. They were very quick to get started and on my way to a perfect smile. 3 months after getting my braces I had my first surgery. That experience was a game changer. The procedure is known as SARPE (surgically assisted rapid palatal expansion) and I‚Äôm not going to sugar coat it, it SUCKED! I was unable to chew anything for 2 months, causing me to lose 25 pounds, it left me with a inch gap in between my two front teeth, and I also had a large very uncomfortable metal device attached to my top teeth holding my jaw together. Needless to say for about 10 months (the total time it took to completely heal) I was immensely regretting my decision. This also led me to have a conversation with Dr. Montano about my apprehension to proceed with the next, more invasive, surgery. But luck was fortunately on my side! Dr. Montano felt the results from my first surgery were better than expected and I would be able to get away without having to do the second procedure. This was amazing news for me to hear and brightened my spirits.
So after 2 years and 3 months and one horrible surgical experience I am happy to say my braces are now off and I am happier than ever. My road to a beautiful smile would not be the same without everyone at the Montano and Cardall office. I cannot speak highly enough of all of them. Dr. Montano and Dr. Cardall were incredible at making me feel that my case was important and it was their mission to provide me with the best care. Every one of the assistants are caring and sympathetic. They took special care of me and I am forever grateful. Anyone who is unhappy with their smile should definitely go see Montano and Cardall orthodontic specialists! It will change your life.<//text>

Lets start by saying that I am very excited about finally finishing up the procedure.

So I wanted to get my teeth aligned for a long time and when I was younger my parents couldn‚Äôt afford it. So it was always put off. Aside from that one of my dentists growing up said to wait until my Wisdom teeth came in so we can see if it'll improve on its own. (It didn‚Äôt).
So fast forward a lot of years and now I decided to pursue a treatment for braces but since I‚Äôm an actor I needed results fast. My sister had a treatment for 2 years and I knew people who had similar results. So I pursued Invisalign since it was supposed to be faster. I was told by one orthodontist I needed to do some jaw alignment so I was skeptical until I found Montano Elevated Orthodontics (previously Montano & Cardall).

After the whole process, which literally was only 12-months, Im very happy with my smile. My family and friends love it. I was always smiling even before the treatment and I will continue smiling after like I always am.

My advice for any future patient you gotta live life smiling. Visit Montano for your orthodontic needs. You will not regret it I promise you!
